focus_tree = {
	id = soviet2_focus
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 300 y = 2000 }

	country = {
		factor = 0

		modifier = {
			add = 1000
			OR = {
				tag = SOV
				tag = SOU
			}
		}

	#The Second Five Year Plan
	focus = {
		id = SOV_start_five_year_plan
		x = 13
		y = 0
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_soviet_construction
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 8
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_start_five_year_plan_tt
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_capital = yes
					is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		completion_reward = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SOV_start_five_year_plan
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = industry
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unhappy_peasants1
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_start_five_year_plans_tt2
			}
		}
	}

	#The Motherland
	focus = {
		id = SOV_the_motherland
		x = 13
		y = 1

		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {

				factor = 100

			}
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
		completion_reward = {
			add_stability = 0.1
		}
	}

		available = {

			}
		}
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_begin_infrastructure_project_tt

		}

	#Great Purge
	focus = {
		id = SOV_great_purge2
		x = 75
		y = 1
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = SOV_avoid_purge focus = SOV_another_revolution }
		icon = GFX_focus_the_purge
		cost = 30
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = RANDOM_COMMUNISM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SOV_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM_DEMOCRATIC
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SOV_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM_NEUTRALITY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SOV_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM_FASCIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_government = communism
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_terrible_fate
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
			}
		}
		select_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.24 days = 1 }
			set_country_flag = SOV_purge_started
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_COMMUNISM_STALIN_RUSSIA }
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_great_purge2_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_great_purge2_tt2
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_ideas = SOV_The_great_officer_purge
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				#Full military purge. Hardest penalty
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
							has_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
						}
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
							has_country_flag = purge_2_group_b
						}
					}
					add_ideas = SOV_The_great_officer_purge
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = soviet.37 days = 146 }
						set_country_flag = no_purgenoncivilwar
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						news_event = { hours = 6 id = news.219 }
					}
				}

				#1 military purge. Lower penalty
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										has_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
										has_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
									}
								}
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
									has_country_flag = purge_2_group_b
								}
							}
							AND = {
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
									has_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
								}
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										has_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
										has_country_flag = purge_2_group_b
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_ideas = SOV_The_great_officer_purge_2
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = soviet.40 days = 146 }
					}
				}

				#No military purge. Lowest penalty.
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
								has_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
								has_country_flag = purge_2_group_b
							}
						}
					}
					add_ideas = SOV_The_great_officer_purge_3
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = soviet.43 days = 146 }
					}
				}
			}

			remove_ideas = SOV_Army_disorganisation
			remove_ideas = trotskyite_plot
			add_ideas = trotskyite_plot_purged

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_other_country = {
							is_major = yes
							has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = soviet.46 days = 3 }
				}
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				division_template = {
					name = "Vozdushno-Desantnaya Brigada"
					is_locked = no
					division_names_group = SOV_PAR_01

					regiments = {
						paratrooper = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						paratrooper = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = nikita_khrushchev
		}
	}

				country_event = { id = soviets.430 days = 5 }
				set_variable = { SOV.sov_track_array_count = 0 }

				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = SOV.sov_track_array_count
							value = 10
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					
					random_scope_in_array = {
						array = global.countries
						limit = {
							exists = yes
							any_state = {
								OR = {
									is_owned_by = THIS
									is_controlled_by = THIS
								}
								is_capital = yes
							}
							NOT = {
								tag = SOV
								has_civil_war = yes
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								has_capitulated = yes
								has_war_with = SOV
								is_subject_of = SOV
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}

						add_to_array = { global.sov_track_available_states = THIS.capital }
						
						add_to_variable = { SOV.sov_track_array_count = 1 }
					}
				}

				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = global.sov_track_available_states
					limit = {}
					
					THIS = {
						set_state_flag = sov_stalin_hidding_state
					}
				}
			}	
		}
	}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { united_russia_strength_minus_one = 1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { stability_add = united_russia_strength_minus_one }

	#The Destiny of Our Monarchy
	focus = {
		id = SOV_destiny_monarchy
		x = 50
		y = 22
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_restoration_tsar }
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_reintegrate_lost_state }
		icon = GFX_goal_tfv_strengthen_commonwealth_ties
		cost = 8
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 7
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = neutrality
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_NEUTRALITY_TSAR_RUSSIA FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
		completion_reward = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.212 days = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_destiny_monarchy_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_destiny_monarchy_tt2

			# 1 = opposed ; 2 = neutral ; 3 = support

			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 1 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 2 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 3 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 4 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 5 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 6 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 7 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 8 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 9 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 10 }

			set_variable = { houses_russia_half_index = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
			    array = monarchy_houses_russia

			    add_to_variable = { houses_russia_half_index = 1 }
			}
			divide_variable = {
			    var = houses_russia_half_index
			    value = 2
			}

			set_variable = { house_russia_opposed = 0 }
			set_variable = { house_russia_neutral = 0 }
			set_variable = { house_russia_support = 0 }
			# set_variable = { debug_house_count = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
			    array = monarchy_houses_russia
			    value = current
			    index = i

				set_temp_variable = { current_value = current }
				set_temp_variable = { current_index = i }
				set_variable = { house_russia^var:current_value = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
						    var = current_index
						    value = houses_russia_half_index
						    compare = less_than
						}
					}
					randomize_variable = {
						var = house_russia^var:current_value
						distribution = uniform
						min = 1
						max = 2
					}
				}
				else = {
					randomize_variable = {
						var = house_russia^var:current_value
						distribution = uniform
						min = 2
						max = 3
					}
				}
				round_variable = house_russia^var:current_value
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 1
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 30 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_opposed
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 2
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 20 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_neutral
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 10 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_support
						value = 1
					}
				}
			    # add_to_variable = { debug_house_count = house_russia@var:current_value }
			}
		}
	}

			else {

				}
				YUG = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
					is_subject = no
					if = {

							}
						}

							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_destroy_communist
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
